 usne mantri ji ko sirf itnaa bataaya tha ki uskaa pehla kartavya yatriyon ke prati he, lekin saamne khadey raajnneetijna ne shikaayat kar daali ki vah 'budtameez' he
 This is the story of an Air India captain who had to face 'VIP strength' to speak on behalf of his passengers
 kya kendriya mantri kiran rigiju tathaa jammu evam kashmir ke upmukhyamantri nirmal singh kii vajah se der se udi air india kii flite eai 446 ke captain rohan sahaaran ko 'bali kaa bakra' banaaya ja rahaa he? NDTV ke paas maujuud exclusive jaankaree kii badaulat bhartiya vayusena dwaara sanchalit leh airport par hue puure drame kaa khulaasa hota he, jo captain sahaaran ke liye 'bure sapane' jaisaa tha
 On the morning of 24 June, when Captain Rohan Saharan arrived in Leh, he was given a 'notice to Airmen Order' (NOTEM), which clearly stated that the airport's runway was to be resurfaced (it was ready for flight) by 11 am, so No flight can leave after 10:35 am
 unhen pataa chalaa ki unhen puri flite ko udaakar waapas le janaa hoga, jabaki airport par pehle se hi hangaame ke asaar the, kyonki concermd tikaton ke saath maujuud teen yatriyon ko tab tak bhi boarding paas jari nahin kiye ja rahe the
 According to sources, he spoke with the local authorities so that these three passengers - an Indian Foreign Service officer and his family - were given their boarding passes
 iske baad unhen soochna sthaneey jila prashasan or police adhikariyon dwaara soochna di gai ki unhen isi udaan main 'teen viipi' ko bhi lekar janaa hoga
 By now, Captain Saharan was beginning to get quite worried
 ek sutara ke mutabik, mausam tab tak 'marginal' ho chukaa tha
 To put it simply, it meant that the weather had begun to heat up, and if it had been a little warmer, the captain would have had to take off luggage and passengers to lighten the plane
 chashmadid gavaahon ke mutabik, ab tak ve teen yatri, jinhen aakhirkaar boarding paas die ja chuke the, taramac par vimaan kii ore jane vaali bas main baithe hue the
 He sat there for an hour, but was not allowed to board the plane
 anya yatri, jo vimaan ke udaan na bharne kii vajah se gusse main the, airline ko kosna shuru kar chuke the
 Eventually, Captain Saharan was given a trim sheet to load and sign - this is the last document the pilot has to sign before taking off - and he orders the doors closed
 unki puri koshishon ke baavjood ve teen yatri taramac par bas main hi baithe the, jinhen sthaneey adhikariyon ne vimaan main nahin chadhane diya
 The vips arrived after the plane doors were closed, and under pressure the captain had to open the doors of the plane for them
 is samay tak vimaan main baithe yatriyon kaa gussa or bad chukaa tha, or unhone 'deree kaa kaaran' bane viipi logon ko hoot karnaa shuru kar diya
 Captain Saharan, pointing to the three passengers still boarding the bus on the Tarmac, told the two politicians, "we have been late for more than an hour and a half because of you guys
"

 " Is it due to Union Minister Kiran Rijiju and Jammu and Kashmir Deputy Chief Minister Nirmal Singh that late Captain Rohan Saharan of Air India Flight AI 446 is being made a 'scapegoat'? Exclusive information possessed by NDTV reveals the entire drama at Leh Airport operated by the Indian Air Force, which was a 'nightmare' for Captain Saharan
 24 june kii subah jab captain rohan sahaaran leh pahunche to unhen 'notice tu airmen order' (NOTEM) diya gaya, jisamen spasht likhaa tha ki airport kaa ranve 11 baje praatah tak riserphes (use udaan ke liye dobaaraa taiyaar) kiya janaa he, atah praatah 10:35 baje ke baad koi udaan nahin ja sakati
 They found out that they would have to fly the entire flight back, while there was already an uproar at the airport as boarding passes were not being issued to the three passengers with confirmed tickets
 sutron ke anusaar, unhone sthaneey adhikariyon ke saath baat kii, taaki in teen yatriyon - ek bhartiya videsh seva adhikari tathaa unka parivaar - ko unke boarding paas de die jaaen
 After this, they were informed by the local district administration and police officials that they would have to take 'three vips' in the same flight
 ab tak, captain sahaaran kaaphi chintit hone lage the
 According to one source, the weather was 'marginal' by then
 sada shabdon main kahen to iskaa arth tha ki mausam garm hone laga tha, or agar yah thodaa bhi or garm hota, to captain ko vimaan ko halkaa karne ke liye saamaan or yatriyon tak ko utaar dena padataa
 According to eyewitnesses, by now three passengers who were finally given boarding passes were sitting in a bus heading to the plane on the tarmac
 ve ek ghante tak vahaan baithe rahe, lekin unhen vimaan main savaar hone kii anumati nahin di gai
 Other passengers, who were furious over the plane not flying, started cursing the airline
 aakhirkaar, captain sahaaran ko lod tathaa sin karne ke liye trim shit de di gai - yah vah aakhri dastauez he, jis par payalat ko udaan bharne se pehle dastakhat karne hote hai - or unhone darvaaze band karne kaa aadesh de diya
 Despite their best efforts, the three passengers were sitting in a bus on the Tarmac, which was not allowed by the local authorities to board the plane
 vimaan ke darvaaze band hone ke baad viipi pahunche, or dabaav main captain ko unke liye vimaan ke darvaaze kholane pade
 By this time, the anger of the passengers boarding the aircraft had increased further, and they started hooting the vips who were the 'cause of delay'
 captain sahaaran ne taramac par tab bhi bas main baithe teen yatriyon kii ore ishaara karte hue donon rajanetaaon se kaha, "ham aap logon kii vajah se dedh ghante se bhi zyaada let ho chuke hai
